8. Fast Chewing For this exercise you need the JAWLINER. Take both JAWLINER pieces, place them on the two back molars and bite quickly. Make sure to not make any rotating chewing movements. Move your jaws just up and down in a controlled manner. Repeat this process 30 times. At first, you won't be able to complete 30 repetitions and your jaw muscles will be exhausted after just a few bites. That's absolutely normal - progress will come over time.
